<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">List of countries by alcohol consumption per capita</h1>
<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
<div id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
<div id="contentSub"></div>
<div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">
					Jump to:					<a href="#mw-head">navigation</a>, 					<a href="#p-search">search</a>
</div>
<div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en"><script>function mfTempOpenSection(id){var block=document.getElementById("mf-section-"+id);block.className+=" open-block";block.previousSibling.className+=" open-block";}</script><p>This is a <b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_countries" title="List of countries">list of countries</a> by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Alcohol_consumption" title="Alcohol consumption">alcohol consumption</a></b> measured in equivalent litres of pure <a href="/wiki/Ethanol" title="Ethanol">ethanol</a> consumed <a href="/wiki/Per_capita" title="Per capita">per capita</a> per year.</p>
<p></p>

<p></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="WHO_Data">WHO Data</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_by_alcohol_consumption_per_capita&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: WHO Data">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The WHO publish periodically The Global Status Report on Alcohol:</p>
<ul>
<li>1999 was first published by WHO in 1999.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup></li>
<li>2004 is the second global status report on alcohol published by WHO</li>
<li>2011 third global report on alcohol published by WHO</li>
<li>2014 fourth global report on alcohol published by WHO with data from 2010</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2010_WHO_data">2010 WHO data</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_by_alcohol_consumption_per_capita&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: 2010 WHO data">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The table below for about 190 countries uses 2010 data from the <a href="/wiki/World_Health_Organization" title="World Health Organization">WHO</a> report published in 2014. The methodology used by the WHO calculated use by persons 15 years of age or older. All data in columns refer to year 2010. The column "recorded" refers to the average recorded consumption for the period 2010. Unrecorded consumption was calculated using empirical investigations and expert judgments. Total is the sum of the recorded and unrecorded consumption. The next four columns are a breakdown of the recorded alcohol consumption by type. <a href="/wiki/Beer" title="Beer">Beer</a> refers to malt beer, <a href="/wiki/Wine" title="Wine">wine</a> refers to grape wine, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Distilled_spirit" title="Distilled spirit">spirits</a> refers to all distilled beverages such as <a href="/wiki/Vodka" title="Vodka">vodka</a> and similar products, and the column "other" refers to all other alcoholic beverages, such as <a href="/wiki/Rice_wine" title="Rice wine">rice wine</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sake" title="Sake">sake</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kumi_kumi" title="Kumi kumi">kumi kumi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kwete" title="Kwete">kwete</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mead" title="Mead">mead</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cider" title="Cider">cider</a>.</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2015_WHO_data_for_OECD_countries">2015 WHO data for OECD countries</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_by_alcohol_consumption_per_capita&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: 2015 WHO data for OECD countries">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The following is a list of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/OECD" title="OECD">OECD</a> countries by the total alcohol consumption <a href="/wiki/Per_capita" title="Per capita">per capita</a> in litres of pure alcohol as published by the <a href="/wiki/World_Health_Organization" title="World Health Organization">World Health Organization</a> in 2015.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup></p>
<table class="wikitable sortable">
<tr>
<th>Rank</th>
<th>Country</th>
<th>Alcohol consumption<br/>
in litres</th>
<th>Relative alcohol consumption</th>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="OECD_Data">OECD Data</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_by_alcohol_consumption_per_capita&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: OECD Data">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2013_OECD_statistics">2013 OECD statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_by_alcohol_consumption_per_capita&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: 2013 OECD statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The table below lists <a href="/wiki/Organisation_for_Economic_Co-operation_and_Development" title="Organisation for Economic Co-operation and Development">OECD</a> countries by the annual consumption of pure alcohol in liters, per person, aged 15 years old and over, as published in the 2013 OECD Health Data. Note that the methodology to convert alcoholic drinks to pure alcohol may differ across countries. Typically beer is weighted as 4–5%, wine as 11–16% and spirits as 40% of pure alcohol equivalent.</p>
<p>This table is an accurate reflection of the annual consumption of pure alcohol in litres by OECD countries.</p>

<tr>
<th class="navbox-group" scope="row" style="text-align:center;">Legality of<br/>
drug use</th>
<td class="navbox-list navbox-even hlist" style="text-align:left;border-left-width:2px;border-left-style:solid;width:100%;padding:0px">
<div style="padding:0em 0.25em"></div>
<table class="nowraplinks navbox-subgroup" style="border-spacing:0">
<tr>
<th class="navbox-group" scope="row" style="padding-left:0;padding-right:0;text-align:center;">
<div style="padding:0em 0.75em;">International</div>
</th>
<td class="navbox-list navbox-even" style="text-align:left;border-left-width:2px;border-left-style:solid;width:100%;padding:0px">
<div style="padding:0em 0.25em">
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Single_Convention_on_Narcotic_Drugs" title="Single Convention on Narcotic Drugs">1961 Narcotic Drugs</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Convention_on_Psychotropic_Substances" title="Convention on Psychotropic Substances">1971 Psychotropic Substances</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Convention_Against_Illicit_Traffic_in_Narcotic_Drugs_and_Psychotropic_Substances" title="United Nations Convention Against Illicit Traffic in Narcotic Drugs and Psychotropic Substances">1988 Drug Trafficking</a></li>
